name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Family Friendly Suite
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:12 Reviews

posted:Posted April 21, 2024
msg:The children wanted to go to the Windmill Park, so they chose the nearest Junlan Resort Hotel. In addition, there was an elderly person, so the parent-child suite was very suitable and the price was very affordable. When booking, it showed that there was no room on Saturday, so they booked one night on Friday. When they checked in, they saw that there was room on Saturday. Then the elderly and children were very satisfied with the room, so they directly renewed the original room for one night.
The hotel is located in Xiangjiadang Scenic Area, with good scenery and environment. It is very close to the Windmill Park and can be reached in a few minutes by car. However, because of its remote location, the surrounding area is relatively quiet and there is no bustling business. It is suitable for self-driving travel. It has its own parking lot and is about 20 minutes drive from the central city of Jiaxing.
The hotel service is also good. If there are any problems, the feedback is relatively timely, and the service staff can keep smiling, which is still worthy of praise. The hotel facilities are also OK. The parent-child suite has a large round bathtub, and the children are very happy at night. The parent-child suite has 2 bathrooms. In addition to the bathtub, there is a shower room. It is equipped with a stepped toilet seat for children, a foot pedal for washing, and children's toothbrushes and slippers are also given when checking in, which is very good. Because it was on the first floor, the room was equipped with electric mosquito coils. We found mosquitoes on the second night, which was just right for us. But there was no refrigerator in the room, which was very inconvenient.
The hotel's breakfast was quite rich and replenished in a timely manner. Overall, it was OK.
As for hygiene, the hotel needs to strengthen management. I won't talk about other things. Just the obvious place like the bedside table, there was so much dust on it (see the video for details), I was shocked, so I didn't think I could look at other places carefully. We just let it go as long as the bed was ok.

posted:Posted April 12, 2024
msg:Qingming Festival is approaching, so I went to Ningbo to visit the graves. I passed by Jiaxing and took a rest at Xiangjia Dang Junlan Resort Hotel in the suburbs of the city.
Xiangjia Dang was a gathering place for literati and scholars in the Ming and Qing Dynasties, where they often recited poems and painted. Today, it is a famous resort in Jiaxing. The lake is wide, the lakeshore is winding, the water is rippling, and the willows on the shore are lined up. Camellias are in full bloom, cherry blossoms are as bright as clouds, and the lake and spring scenery are intoxicating. It is really "the fragrant March in Jiangnan".
The hotel is nestled on the lakeshore, surrounded by green trees and flowers. Staying here, the cold and curling up of a winter are gone...

msg:The location of the hotel is relatively remote, suitable for self-driving, and you can order takeaway. There are above-ground and underground parking lots with sufficient parking spaces, but there are no charging piles.
The decoration of the hotel is in the style of the Republic of China. Maybe most people don't like the style. It is warmer than sleeping. The facilities can only be said to be average, and the maintenance is not good. There are several holes in the bedding. The most speechless thing is that the air conditioner is not cooling enough. I reported to the front desk who knows the way, and I knew at a glance that the air conditioner filter was not cleaned for a long time. Go in, and there are children! There is also a problem that is obviously universal. The customer service has dealt with it more than once. Why not clean up all the filters in the hotel as a whole, but wait for feedback from the guests!
The soundproofing of the room is not very good. The guests upstairs kept moving their chairs for some reason and made a lot of noise all night. There are not many varieties of breakfast, but it is enough to eat, and some common ones are available.
Generally speaking, accommodation is not recommended. First of all, the style of the Republic of China is not suitable for most people. In addition, considering the poor hygiene conditions, be careful when bringing children!
